Apastamba-Grhyasutra,
with Haradatta's Anakula
and Sudarsana's Grhyatatparyadarsana


Input by members of the Sansknet project



This GRETIL version has been converted from a custom Devanagari encoding
with partly inconsistent segmentation of words and phrases.
The text is not proof-read!



STRUCTURE OF REFERENCES (added):
âpGs_nn.nn = âpastamba-Gçhyasåtra_khaõóa.såtra (pañala-numbering ignored)
âpGs-Anà_nn.nn = Haradatta's Anàkulàvçtti
âpGs-Tàt_nn.nn = Sudar÷ana's Gçhyatàtparyadar÷anavyàkhyà

tataþ pariùecanàntaü tantra÷ùaü karoti /
÷amyàþ paridhyarthe iti pårvamevoktam /
kecit-àjyabhàgànta ityanena tantrapràptau siddhàyàmagnerupasamàdhànàdivacanamagnimàtrasyopasamàdhànàrtham /
tenaupàsana÷ånyasyedaü karma laukike 'pi bhavati /

%<abhimçtà>%abhimukhyena mçtà yogyatayà jãvanta eva amàtyànàü santatamaraõadar÷anena svayamapi maraõàdbhãtà ityarthaþ /
tebhyastadartha santatamaraõabhayanivçttyarta%<uttarayà>%'imaü jãvebhyaþ' ityanayà%<paridhiü>% mçtyorantardhànabhåtaü%<a÷mànaü dakùiõato>% nidadhàti /
etacca tantra÷eùànte, kçtveti ktvàpratyayabalàt /
kecit-nidadhàti pratiùñhàpayati /
paridhivacanàcca tasyà÷manaþ pracyàvanaü na kartavyamiti /
